The average contract length is roughly 3 months. Futures contracts are usually inclusive of any interest amounts.\r\nOption Trade - A foreign exchange option (commonly shortened to just FX option) is a derivative where the owner has the right but not the obligation to exchange money denominated in one currency into another currency at a pre-agreed exchange rate on a specified date.\r\nLibor - The London Interbank Offered Rate is the average interest rate estimated by leading banks in London that the average leading bank would be charged if borrowing from other banks.
